style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 90.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第十六条 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同中存在可变对价的，企业应当按照期望值或最可能发生金额确定可变对价的最佳估计数，但包含可变对价的交易价格，应当不超过在相关不确定性消除时累计已确认收入极可能不会发生重大转回的金额。企业在评估累计已确认收入是否</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">极可能不会发生重大转回时，应当同时考虑收入转回的可能性及其比重。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">每一资产负债表日，企业应当重新估计应计入交易价格的可变对价金额。可变对价金额发生变动的，按照本准则第二十四条和第二十五条规定进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.7pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第十七条 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同中存在重大融资成分的，企业应当按照假定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">客户在取得商品控制权时即以现金支付的应付金额确定交易价</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">格。该交易价格与合同对价之间的差额，应当在合同期间内采用</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">实际利率法摊销。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.95pt 5.8pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同开始日，企业预计客户取得商品控制权与客户支付价款</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">间隔不超过一年的，可以不考虑合同中存在的重大融资成分。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第十八条 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">客户支付非现金对价的，企业应当按照非现金对价的公允价值确定交易价格。非现金对价的公允价值不能合理估计的，企业应当参照其承诺向客户转让商品的单独售价间接确定交易价格。非现金对价的公允价值因对价形式以外的原因而发生变动的，应当作为可变对价，按照本准则第十六条规定进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 0cm 6pt 35.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">单独售价，是指企业向客户单独销售商品的价格。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 4.1pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第十九条 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业应付客户（或向客户购买本企业商品的第三方，本条下同）对价的，应当将该应付对价冲减交易价格，并在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">确认相关收入与支付（或承诺支付）客户对价二者孰晚的时点冲减当期收入，但应付客户对价是为了向客户取得其他可明确区分商品的除外。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 5.65pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业应付客户对价是为了向客户取得其他可明确区分商品</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">的，应当采用与本企业其他采购相一致的方式确认所购买的商</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">品。企业应付客户对价超过向客户取得可明确区分商品公允价值</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">的，超过金额应当冲减交易价格。向客户取得的可明确区分商品</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">公允价值不能合理估计的，企业应当将应付客户对价全额冲减交易价格。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二十条 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同中包含两项或多项履约义务的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>企业应当在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同开始<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">日</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>按照各单项履约义务所承诺商品的单独售<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">价</SPAN>的相对</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">比<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">例</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.2pt">，</SPAN>将交易价格分摊至各单项履约义务<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.15pt">。</SPAN>企业不得因合同开始</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">日之后单独售价的变动而重新分摊交易价格。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">十</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">一</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 1.25pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">业在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">类</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">似</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">环</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">境</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">下</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">向</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">类</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">似</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">客</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">户</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">单</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">独</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">销售商</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">品的价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">格</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.2pt">，</SPAN>应作为确定该商品单独售价的最佳证据<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.2pt">。</SPAN>单独售价无法<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">直</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">接</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">观</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">察的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">企</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">业</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">应</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">综合</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">考</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.55pt">虑</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">能</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.5pt">够</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">合理</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">取</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">得</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">全</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt">部</SPAN><SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt">相关</SPAN>信息<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">，</SPAN>采用市<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">场</SPAN>调整法<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">、</SPAN>成本加成法<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -1.45pt">、</SPAN>余值法等方法合理估计单独售价<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.2pt">。</SPAN>在估计单独售价时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -2.2pt">，</SPAN>企业应当最大限度地采用可观察的输入<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">值</SPAN>，并对类似的情况采用一致的估计方<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">法</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.75pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">市场调整法<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>是指企业根据某商品或类似商品的市场售价考</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">虑</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">本企业的成本和毛利等进行适当调整后<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>确定其单独售价的方法。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.75pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">成本加成法，是指企业根据某商品的预计成本加上其合理毛利后的价格，确定其单独售价的方法。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpLast 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.75pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">余值法，是指企业根据合同交易价格减去合同中其他商品可观察的单独售价后的余值，确定某商品单独售价的方法。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 9.0pt"><o:p><FONT 
size=3 face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpFirst 
style="MARGIN: auto 12.75pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二十二条 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业在商品近期售价波动幅度巨大<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>或者因未</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">定价且未<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">曾</SPAN>单独销售而使售价无法可靠确定时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>可采用余值法估计其单独售<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">价</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 12.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二十三条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对于合同折扣<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>企业应当在各单项履约义务之间按比例分<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">摊</SPAN>。</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 12.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">有确凿证据表明合同折扣仅与合同中一项或多项（而非全</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">部）履约义务相关的，企业应当将该合同折扣分摊至相关一项或</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">多项履约义务。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同折扣仅与合同中一项或多项（而非全部）履约义务相关，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">且企业采用余值法估计单独售价的，应当首先按照前款规定在该一项或多项（而非全部）履约义务之间分摊合同折扣，然后采用余值法估计单独售价。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 12.8pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同折扣，是指合同中各单项履约义务所承诺商品的单独售价之和高于合同交易价格的金额。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 12.8pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二十四条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对于可变对价及可变对价的后续变动额，企业</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">应当按照本准则第二十条至第二十三条规定，将其分摊至与之相</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">关的一项或多项履约义务，或者分摊至构成单项履约义务的一系</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">列可明确区分商品中的一项或多项商品。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 12.8pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对于已履行的履约义务，其分摊的可变对价后续变动额应当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">调整变动当期的收入。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 12.8pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二十五条<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同变更之后发生可变对价后续变动的，企业应当区分下列三种情形分别进行会计处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 5.65pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）合同变更属于本准则第八条（一）规定情形的，企业</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">应当判断可变对价后续变动与哪一项合同相关，并按照本准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">二十四条规定进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）合同变更属于本准则第八条（二）规定情形，且可变</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对价后续变动与合同变更前已承诺可变对价相关的，企业应当首</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">先将该可变对价后续变动额以原合同开始日确定的基础进行分</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">摊，然后再将分摊至合同变更日尚未履行履约义务的该可变对价</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">后续变动额以新合同开始日确定的基础进行二次分摊。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpLast 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（三）合同变更之后发生除本条（一）、（二）规定情形以外</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">的可变对价后续变动的，企业应当将该可变对价后续变动额分摊</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">至合同变更日尚未履行的履约义务。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0.1pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 18pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 14.0pt"><o:p><FONT 
face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyText 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 6pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 59.95pt" 
align=center><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四章<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN>合同成本<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p><FONT 
face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpFirst 
style="MARGIN: auto 5.65pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二十六条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业为履行合同发生的成本<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>不属于其他企业</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">会计准则<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -0.05pt">规</SPAN>范范围且同时满足下列条件的<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>应<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">当</SPAN>作为合同履约成</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">本确认为一项资产：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）该成本与一份当前或预期取得的合同直接相关，包括</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">直接人工、直接材料、制造费用（或类似费用）、明确由客户承</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">担的成本以及仅因该合同而发生的其他成本；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）该成本增加了企业未来用于履行履约义务的资源；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（三）该成本预期能够收回。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto auto auto 35.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 105.0pt; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二十七条<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业应当在下列支出发生时<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -4.45pt">，</SPAN>将其计入当期损益：</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）管理费用。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）非正常消耗的直接材料、直接人工和制造费用（或类</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">似费用），这些支出为履行合同发生，但未反映在合同价格中。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（三）与履约义务中已履行部分相关的支出。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（四）无法在尚未履行的与已履行的履约义务之间区分的相关支出。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 9.4pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.3pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">十</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">八</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 1.4pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业为取得合同发生的增量成本预期能够收回的，应当作为合同取得成本确认为一项资产；但是，该资产摊销期限不超过一年的，可以在发生时计入当期损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.95pt 9.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">增量成本，是指企业不取得合同就不会发生的成本（如销售</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">佣金等）。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 9.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业为取得合同发生的、除预期能够收回的增量成本之外的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">其他支出（如无论是否取得合同均会发生的差旅费等），应当在</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">发生时计入当期损益，但是，明确由客户承担的除外。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 2.95pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 81.05pt 117.6pt; mso-add-space: auto" 
align=left><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第二</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">十</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">九</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">条<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-spacerun: yes">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">按照本准则第二十六条和第二十八条规定确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">认的资产（以下简称</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>“</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">与合同成本有关的资产</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>”</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">），应当采用与该</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">资产相关的商品收入确认相同的基础进行摊销，计入当期损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> <SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></FONT></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 2.95pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 81.05pt 117.6pt; mso-add-space: auto" 
align=left><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十条<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN 
style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">与合同成本有关的资产，其账面价值高于下列两</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">项的差额的，超出部分应当计提减值准备，并确认为资产减值损失：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）企业因转让与该资产相关的商品预期能够取得的剩余对价；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）为转让该相关商品估计将要发生的成本。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">以前期间减值的因素之后发生变化，使得前款（一）减（二）的差额高于该资产账面价值的，应当转回原已计提的资产减值准</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">备，并计入当期损益，但转回后的资产账面价值不应超过假定不</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">计提减值准备情况下该资产在转回日的账面价值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 2.95pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 81.05pt 117.6pt; mso-add-space: auto" 
align=left><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十一条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">在确定与合同成本有关的资产的减值损失时，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业应当首先对按照其他相关企业会计准则确认的、与合同有关</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">的其他资产确定减值损失；然后，按照本准则第三十条规定确定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">与合同成本有关的资产的减值损失。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 2.95pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 81.05pt 117.6pt; mso-add-space: auto" 
align=left><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业按照《企业会计准则第８号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">资产减值》测试相关资</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">产组的减值情况时，应当将按照前款规定确定与合同成本有关的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">资产减值后的新账面价值计入相关资产组的账面价值。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: auto 6.9pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 59.95pt; mso-add-space: auto" 
align=center><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第五章<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN>特定交易的会计处理<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: 2.95pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 81.05pt 117.6pt; mso-add-space: auto" 
align=left><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十二条 
</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对于附有销售退回条款的销售，企业应当在客</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">户取得相关商品控制权时，按照因向客户转让商品而预期有权收</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">取的对价金额（即，不包含预期因销售退回将退还的金额）确认</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">收入，按照预期因销售退回将退还的金额确认负债；同时，按照</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">预期将退回商品转让时的账面价值，扣除收回该商品预计发生的</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">成本（包括退回商品的价值减损）后的余额，确认为一项资产，按照所转让商品转让时的账面价值，扣除上述资产成本的净额结转成本。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">每一资产负债表日，企业应当重新估计未来销售退回情况，</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">如有变化，应当作为会计估计变更进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.15pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 94.5pt; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十三条<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对于附有质量保证条款的销售，企业应当评估该质量保证是否在向客户保证所销售商品符合既定标准之外提供了一项单独的服务。企业提供额外服务的，应当作为单项履约义务，按照本准则规定进行会计处理；否则，质量保证责任应当</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> 13</FONT> </SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">或有事项》规定进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">在评估质量保证是否在向客户保证所销售商品符合既定标准之</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">外提供了一项单独的服务时，企业应当考虑该质量保证是否为法定要求、质量保证期限以及企业承诺履行任务的性质等因素。客</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">户能够选择单独购买质量保证的，该质量保证构成单项履约义务。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 3.25pt 5.25pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 94.6pt; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">十</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">四</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">条<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业应当根据其在向客户转让商品前是否拥</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">有对该商品的控制权，来判断其从事交易时的身份是主要责任人还是代理人。企业在向客户转让商品前能够控制该商品的，该企业为主要责任人，应当按照已收或应收对价总额确认收入；否则，该企业为代理人，应当按照预期有权收取的佣金或手续费的金额确认收入，该金额应当按照已收或应收对价总额扣除应支付给其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">他相关方的价款后的净额，或者按照既定的佣金金额或比例等确定。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 0cm 6pt 35.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业向客户转让商品前能够控<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">制</SPAN>该商品的情形包括：</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）企业自第三方取得商品或其他资产控制权后，再转让给客户。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）企业能够主导第三方代表本企业向客户提供服务。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（三）企业自第三方取得商品控制权后，通过提供重大的服</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">务将该商品与其他商品整合成某组合产出转让给客户。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">在具体判断向客户转让商品前是否拥有对该商品的控制权时，企业不应仅局限于合同的法律形式，而应当综合考虑所有相</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">关事实和情况，这些事实和情况包括：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）企业承担向客户转让商品的主要责任。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）企业在转让商品之前或之后承担了该商品的存货风</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">险。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（三）企业有权自主决定所交易商品的价格。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（四）其他相关事实和情况。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: left; MARGIN: auto 5.3pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 94.5pt; mso-add-space: auto" 
align=left><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十五条<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对于附有客户额外购买选择权的销售，企业应</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">当评估该选择权是否向客户提供了一项重大权利。企业提供重大权利的，应当作为单项履约义务，按照本准则第二十条至第二十四条规定将交易价格分摊至该履约义务，在客户未来行使购买选择权取得相关商品控制权时，或者该选择权失效时，确认相应的收入。客户额外购买选择权的单独售价无法直接观察的，企业应</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">当综合考虑客户行使和不行使该选择权所能获得的折扣的差异、客户行使该选择权的可能性等全部相关信息后，予以合理估计。客户虽然有额外购买商品选择权，但客户行使该选择权购买商品时的价格反映了这些商品单独售价的，不应被视为企业向该客户提供了一项重大权利。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 36pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto; mso-char-indent-count: 3.0"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十六条<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp; </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业向客户授予知识产权许可的，应当按照本准则第九条和第十条规定评估该知识产权许可是否构成单项履约义务，构成单项履约义务的，应当进一步确定其是在某一时段</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">内履行还是在某一时点履行。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业向客户授予知识产权许可，同时满足下列条件时，应当作为在某一时段内履行的履约义务确认相关收入；否则，应当作为在某一时点履行的履约义务确认相关收入：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）合同要求或客户能够合理预期企业将从事对该项知识</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">产权有重大影响的活动；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）该活动对客户将产生有利或不利影响；</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（三）该活动不会导致向客户转让某项商品。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 5.65pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十七条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业向客户授予知识产权许可，并约定按客户实际销售或使用情况收取特许权使用费的，应当在下列两项孰晚的时点确认收入：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US
