style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 0cm 6pt 35.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）客户后续销售或使用行为实际发<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.05pt">生</SPAN>；</SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto auto auto 35.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）企业履行相关履约义务。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 5.65pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十八条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对于售后回购交易，企业应当区分下列两种情</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">形分别进行会计处理：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.7pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）企业因存在与客户的远期安排而负有回购义务或企业享有回购权利的，表明客户在销售时点并未取得相关商品控制权，企业应当作为租赁交易或融资交易进行相应的会计处理。其</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">中，回购价格低于原售价的，应当视为租赁交易，按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>21</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">租赁》的相关规定进行会计处理；回购价格不低于原售价的，应当视为融资交易，在收到客户款项时确认金融负债，并将该款项和回购价格的差额在回购期间内确认为利息</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">费用等。企业到期未行使回购权利的，应当在该回购权利到期时终止确认金融负债，同时确认收入。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.7pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）企业负有应客户要求回购商品义务的，应当在合同开</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">始日评估客户是否具有行使该要求权的重大经济动因。客户具有行使该要求权重大经济动因的，企业应当将售后回购作为租赁交易或融资交易，按照本条（一）规定进行会计处理；否则，企业应当将其作为附有销售退回条款的销售交易，按照本准则第三十二条规定进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.7pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">售后回购，是指企业销售商品的同时承诺或有权选择日后再将该商品（包括相同或几乎相同的商品，或以该商品作为组成部分的商品）购回的销售方式。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.3pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第三十九条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业向客户预收销售商品款项的，应当首先将该款项确认为负债，待履行了相关履约义务时再转为收入。当企业预收款项无需退回，且客户可能会放弃其全部或部分合同权利</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">时，企业预期将有权获得与客户所放弃的合同权利相关的金额的，应当按照客户行使合同权利的模式按比例将上述金额确认为收入；否则，企业只有在客户要求其履行剩余履约义务的可能性极低时，才能将上述负债的相关余额转为收入。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 0.15pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业在合同开始（或接近合同开始）日向客户收</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">取的无需退回的初始费（如俱乐部的入会费等）应当计入交易价格。企业应当评估该初始费是否与向客户转让已承诺的商品相关。该初始费与向客户转让已承诺的商品相关，并且该商品构成单项履约义务的，企业应当在转让该商品时，按照分摊至该商品的交易价格确认收入；该初始费与向客户转让已承诺的商品相关，但该商品不构成单项履约义务的，企业应当在包含该商品的单项履约义务履行时，按照分摊至该单项履约义务的交易价格确认收入；该初始费与向客户转让已承诺的商品不相关的，该初始费应当作为未来将转让商品的预收款，在未来转让该商品时确认为收入。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.6pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业收取了无需退回的初始费且为履行合同应开展初始活动，但这些活动本身并没有向客户转让已承诺的商品的，该初始费与未来将转让的已承诺商品相关，应当在未来转让该商品时确认为收入，企业在确定履约进度时不应考虑这些初始活动；企业为该初始活动发生的支出应当按照本准则第二十六条和第二十七条规定确认为一项资产或计入当期损益。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpLast 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: auto auto auto 0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 60.1pt 90.1pt; mso-add-space: auto" 
align=center><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第六章<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN>列<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN>报<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0.3pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 11pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 10.0pt"><o:p><FONT 
face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpFirst 
style="MARGIN: auto 5.65pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">十</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">一</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 1.35pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业应当根据本企业履行履约义务与客户付款之间的关系在资产负债表中列示合同资产或合同负债。企业拥有的、无条件（即，仅取决于时间流逝）向客户收取对价的权利</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">应当作为应收款项单独列示。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同资产，是指企业已向客户转让商品而有权收取对价的权利，且该权利取决于时间流逝之外的其他因素。如企业向客户销售两项可明确区分的商品，企业因已交付其中一项商品而有权收取款项，但收取该款项还取决于企业交付另一项商品的，企业应</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">当将该收款权利作为合同资产。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">合同负债，是指企业已收或应收客户对价而应向客户转让商</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">品的义务。如企业在转让承诺的商品之前已收取的款项。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpLast 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">按照本准则确认的合同资产的减值的计量和列报应当按照《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> 22</FONT> </SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">金融工具确认和计量》和《企业会计准则第</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> 37</FONT> </SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">号</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>——</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">金融工具列报》的规定进行会计处理。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0.45pt 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 7.5pt"><o:p><FONT 
face=Calibri>&nbsp;</FONT></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpFirst 
style="MARGIN: auto 12.7pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 106.1pt; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">十</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">二</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">条<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1"> </SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业应当在附注中披露与收入有关的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 12.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（一）收入确认和计量所采用的会计政策、对于确定收入确</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">认的时点和金额具有重大影响的判断以及这些判断的变更，包括</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">确定履约进度的方法及采用该方法的原因、评估客户取得所转让</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">商品控制权时点的相关判断，在确定交易价格、估计计入交易价</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">格的可变对价、分摊交易价格以及计量预期将退还给客户的款项</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">等类似义务时所采用的方法、输入值和假设等。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.95pt 0cm 6pt 35.9pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（二）与合同相关的下列信息：</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>1.</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">与本期确认收入相关的信息，包括与客户之间的合同产</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">生的收入、该收入按主要类别（如商品类型、经营地区、市场或</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">客户类型、合同类型、商品转让的时间、合同期限、销售渠道等）分解的信息以及该分解信息与每一报告分部的收入之间的关系等。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>2.</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">与应收款项、合同资产和合同负债的账面价值相关的信息，包括与客户之间的合同产生的应收款项、合同资产和合同负债的期初和期末账面价值、对上述应收款项和合同资产确认的减值损失、在本期确认的包括在合同负债期初账面价值中的收入、前期已经履行（或部分履行）的履约义务在本期调整的收入、履行履约义务的时间与通常的付款时间之间的关系以及此类因素对合同资产和合同负债账面价值的影响的定量或定性信息、合同资产和合同负债的账面价值在本期内发生的重大变动情况等。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>3.</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">与履约义务相关的信息，包括履约义务通常的履行时间、</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">重要的支付条款、企业承诺转让的商品的性质（包括说明企业是</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">否作为代理人）、企业承担的预期将退还给客户的款项等类似义</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">务、质量保证的类型及相关义务等。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.95pt 5.25pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体>4.</FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">与分摊至剩余履约义务的交易价格相关的信息，包括分摊至本期末尚未履行（或部分未履行）履约义务的交易价格总额、上述金额确认为收入的预计时间的定量或定性信息、未包括在交易价格的对价金额（如可变对价）等。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.95pt 5.25pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（三）与合同成本有关的资产相关的信息，包括确定该资产金额所做的判断、该资产的摊销方法、按该资产主要类别（如为取得合同发生的成本、为履行合同开展的初始活动发生的成本等）披露的期末账面价值以及本期确认的摊销及减值损失金额等。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.95pt 5.25pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">（四）企业根据本准则第十七条规定因预计客户取得商品控制权与客户支付价款间隔未超过一年而未考虑合同中存在的重大融资成分，或者根据本准则第二十八条规定因合同取得成本的摊销期限未超过一年而将其在发生时计入当期损益的，应当披露该事实。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 59.95pt" 
align=center><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第七章<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN>衔接规定<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: auto 5.65pt auto auto; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四十三条</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">首次执行本准则的企业，应当根据首次执行本准则的累积影响数，调整首次执行本准则当年年初留存收益及财</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">务报表其他相关项目金额，对可比期间信息不予调整。企业可以仅对在首次执行日尚未完成的合同的累积影响数进行调整。同时，企业应当在附注中披露，与收入相关会计准则制度的原规定</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">相比，执行本准则对当期财务报表相关项目的影响金额，如有重大影响的，还需披露其原因。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">已完成的合同，是指企业按照与收入相关会计准则制度的原</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">规定已完成合同中全部商品的转让的合同。尚未完成的合同，是</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">指除已完成的合同之外的其他合同。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.5pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第四</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.35pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">十</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LETTER-SPACING: 0.45pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">四</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">条<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: 1.35pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">对于最早可比期间期初之前或首次执行本准</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">则当年年初之前发生的合同变更，企业可予以简化处理，即无需按照本准则第八条规定进行追溯调整，而是根据合同变更的最终安排，识别已履行的和尚未履行的履约义务、确定交易价格以及在已履行的和尚未履行的履约义务之间分摊交易价格。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpMiddle 
style="MARGIN: 2.9pt 5.65pt 6pt 0cm; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; TEXT-INDENT: 29.95pt; mso-mirror-indents: yes; mso-add-space: auto"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">企业采用该简化处理方法的，应当对所有合同一致采用，并</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=宋体> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">且在附注中披露该事实以及在合理范围内对采用该简化处理方法的影响所作的定性分析。</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><o:p></o:p></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoBodyTextCxSpLast 
style="TEXT-ALIGN: center; MARGIN: auto auto auto 0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes; tab-stops: 60.1pt 90.1pt; mso-add-space: auto" 
align=center><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体">第八章<SPAN 
lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN>附<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN>则<SPAN lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></SPAN></SPAN></P>
<P class=MsoNormal 
style="MARGIN: 0cm 0cm 0pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-mirror-indents: yes"><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 黑体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 黑体"><FONT 
face=Calibri>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</FONT>第四十五条<SPAN lang=EN-US><SPAN style="mso-tab-count: 1">&nbsp;&nbsp; 
</SPAN></SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">本准则自</SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; LETTER-SPACING: -3.7pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt"><FONT 
face=Calibri> </FONT></SPAN><SPAN lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; LETTER-SPACING: -0.1pt; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 仿宋">2</SPAN><SPAN 
lang=EN-US 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 仿宋; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 仿宋">018<SPAN 
style="LETTER-SPACING: -3.85pt"> </SPAN></SPAN><SPAN 
style="FONT-SIZE: 12pt; FONT-FAMILY: 宋体; LINE-HEIGHT: 150%; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt">年</SPAN><SPAN
